19:54
‚ÄúThe only tried and true method to gather the location data from the controllers is to combine the data from the gyroscopes and accelerometers with at least one camera, a la PS4, or more commonly multiple cameras like on PC with Oculus and the like. They're starting to use cameras mounted on the VR headset itself, but they're still not able to see the controllers sometimes and you really need a super fast, and super accurate method for a game like this. The problem with only using the hardware in the controllers is that they very easily lose track of themselves after being moved around quickly, and need something external to reference to sync back up. The Wii used to combine the sensor bar with the gyro in the Wii motion plus to accomplish this, but no current system employs one, and the closest thing is the right joycon with it's ir camera.
